Library\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n</ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Museums_and_galleries">Museums and galleries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Museums and galleries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3664" data-file-width="2748" decoding="async" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG/220px-Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG/330px-Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG/440px-Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Fachada_museo_nacional.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>National Museum of Colombia</div></div></div>\n<p>The city offers 58 museums and over 70 art galleries.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The <a href="/wiki/Colombian_National_Museum" title="Colombian National Museum">Colombian National Museum</a> has acquisitions divided into four collections: art, history, archeology and ethnography. The <a href="/wiki/Gold_Museum,_Bogot%C3%A1" title="Gold Museum, Bogot&#225;">Gold Museum</a>, with 35,000 pieces of tumbaga gold, along with 30,000 objects in ceramic, stone and textiles, represents the largest collection of pre-Columbian gold in the world.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Botero_Museum" title="Botero Museum">Botero Museum</a> has 123 works of Fernando Botero and 87 works by international artists. The Museum of Modern Art in Bogot&#225; has a collection of graphic arts, industrial design and photography. The Museum of Colonial Art is home to an important collection of colonial art from Colombia. Fundaci&#243;n Gilberto Alzate Avenda&#241;o hosts activities related to the performing arts and shows temporary exhibits of art in its halls and galleries.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>Among the scientific museums are the Archeological Museum &#8211; Casa del Marqu&#233;s de San Jorge, which has about 30 thousand pieces of pre-Columbian art, Instituto de Ciencias Naturales (UN), one of the four largest museums of natural sciences in Latin America, and the Geological Museum, which has a collection specializing in Geology and Paleontology.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>Bogot&#225; has historical museums like the <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Eliecer_Gaitan_Museum" title="Jorge Eliecer Gaitan Museum">Jorge Eliecer Gaitan Museum</a>, the Museum of Independence (Museo de la Independencia), the <a href="/wiki/Quinta_de_Bol%C3%ADvar" title="Quinta de Bol&#237;var">Quinta de Bol&#237;var</a> and the Casa Museo Francisco Jos&#233; de Caldas, as well as the headquarters of Maloka and the <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_Museum_of_Bogot%C3%A1" title="Children\'s Museum of Bogot&#225;">Children\'s Museum of Bogot&#225;</a>. New museums include the Art Deco and the Museum of Bogot&#225;.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Theater_and_arts">Theater and arts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Theater and arts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FITB.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="744" decoding="async" height="262" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/FITB.jpg/190px-FITB.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/FITB.jpg/285px-FITB.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/FITB.jpg/380px-FITB.jpg 2x" width="190"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FITB.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ibero-American_Theater_Festival" title="Ibero-American Theater Festival">Ibero-American Theater Festival</a></div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Picolontheaterj.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/af/Picolontheaterj.jpg/220px-Picolontheaterj.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/a/af/Picolontheaterj.jpg 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Picolontheaterj.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Teatro_de_Crist%C3%B3bal_Col%C3%B3n" title="Teatro de Crist&#243;bal Col&#243;n">Teatro de Crist&#243;bal Col&#243;n</a></i> (Christopher Columbus Theater)</div></div></div>\n<p>Besides the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ibero-American_Theater_Festival" title="Ibero-American Theater Festival">Ibero-American Theater Festival</a>, the largest theater festival in the world, the city has forty-five theaters; the principal ones are the <a href="/wiki/Teatro_de_Crist%C3%B3bal_Col%C3%B3n" title="Teatro de Crist&#243;bal Col&#243;n">Colon Theater</a>, the newly built <a class="extiw" href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioteca_P%C3%BAblica_Julio_Mario_Santo_Domingo" title="es:Biblioteca P&#250;blica Julio Mario Santo Domingo">Teatro Mayor Julio Mario Santo Domingo</a>, the National Theater with its two venues, the traditional TPB Hall, the Theater of La Candelaria, the Camarin del Carmen (over 400 years old, formerly a convent), the Colsubsidio, and a symbol of the city, the renovated <a class="extiw" href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teatro_Jorge_Eli%C3%A9cer_Gait%C3%A1n" title="es:Teatro Jorge Eli&#233;cer Gait&#225;n">Teatro Jorge Eliecer Gaitan</a>, Le&#243;n de Greiff Auditorium (home of the Bogot&#225; Philharmonic Orchestra), and the Open Air Theater "La Media Torta", where musical events are also held.\n</p><p>The Ibero-American Theater Festival, is not the only acclaimed festival. There are many other regional and local theater festivals that are celebrated and maintain the city active year-round . Amongst the most populars is "The Alternative Theater Festival".\n</p><p>Bogot&#225; has its own film festival, the <a href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1_Film_Festival" title="Bogot&#225; Film Festival">Bogot&#225; Film Festival</a>, and many theaters, showing both contemporary films and art cinema. Bogota\'s international art fair, <a href="/wiki/ArtBo" title="ArtBo">ArtBo</a>, takes place in October of every year and showcases thousands of works covering arts across all formats, movements, and concepts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The main cultural center of the city is the La Candelaria, historic center of the city, with a concentration of universities and museums. In 2007 Bogot&#225; was designated the Ibero-American cultural Capital of Iberoamerica.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Before the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_conquest_of_the_Muisca" title="Spanish conquest of the Muisca">Spanish conquest</a>, the beliefs of the inhabitants of Bogot&#225; formed part of the <a href="/wiki/Muisca_religion" title="Muisca religion">Muisca religion</a>. From the colonial period onwards, the city has been predominantly Roman Catholic. Proof of this religious tradition is the number of churches built in the historic city center. The city has been seat of the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Bogot%C3%A1" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Bogot&#225;">Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Bogot&#225;</a> since 22 March 1564. The seat of the Archbishop is the <a href="/wiki/Primatial_Cathedral_of_Bogot%C3%A1" title="Primatial Cathedral of Bogot&#225;">Primatial Cathedral of Bogot&#225;</a>; the archdiocese itself is located in new buildings in the north of the city. However a large group of the population nowadays declares itself non-practicing.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>The city has a mosque located in the area of Chapinero called the Estambul mosque,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> a mosque being built on the Calle 80 with Cra 30 called Abou Bakr Alsiddiq mosque<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup> and which is the first in the city to have the traditional Islamic architecture, and an Islamic Center called Al-Qurtubi.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The main <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ashkenazi" title="Ashkenazi">Ashkenazi</a> Jewish synagogue (there are a total of 4 synagogues in Bogot&#225;) is located on 94th street (also called State of Israel avenue).\n</p><p>An Eastern Orthodox church and the San Pablo Anglican Cathedral, the mother church of the Episcopal Church in Colombia, are both located in Chapinero. The <a href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1_Colombia_Temple" title="Bogot&#225; Colombia Temple">Bogot&#225; Colombia Temple</a> of <a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints">The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints</a> is located in the Niza neighborhood. There are four Buddhist centers located in the north of the city. There is also a wide variety of Protestant churches in different parts of the city, including the Bogot&#225; Baptist Chapel, the non-denominational Union Church, and the St. Matthaus Evangelical Lutheran Church which holds services in German as well as Spanish for the German-Colombian community.\n</p>\n<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Torre_central_de_la_iglesia_de_Lourdes_en_Bogot%C3%A1.JPG"><img alt="" data-file-height="2815" data-file-width="3753" decoding="async" height="120" class="thumb" style="width: 218px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:El_Lugar_de_Su_Presencia_Exterior.png"><img alt="" data-file-height="2440" data-file-width="4424" class="gallerytext">\n<p><a href="/wiki/Protestantism" title="Protestantism">Protestant</a> <a href="/wiki/Megachurch" title="Megachurch">Megachurch</a>\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Iglesia_SUD_en_Bogot%C3%A1.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" decoding="async" height="120" Colombia Mormon Temple\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 156.66666666667px"><div style="width: 156.66666666667px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 154.66666666667px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:View_from_the_local_Transmilenio_of_the_Abou_Bakr_Alsiddiq_Mosque_2013.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="206" Bakr Alsiddiq Mosque\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n</ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There is a broad array of restaurants in Bogot&#225; that serve typical and international food. Parque de la 93, Usaqu&#233;n, Zona T, The <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=G_Zone&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="G Zone (page does not exist)">G Zone</a>, La Macarena, La Candelaria and the International Center are some of the main sectors where a number of international restaurants are found, ranging from Argentinian, Peruvian, Venezuelan, Brazilian, Mexican, American establishments to Arabic, Asian, French, Italian, Russian and British bistros, rotisseries, steakhouses and pubs, just to name a few.\nTypical dishes of Bogot&#225; include the <a href="/wiki/Ajiaco" title="Ajiaco">ajiaco</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> a soup prepared with chicken, a variety of potatoes, corn on the cob, and <i><a href="/wiki/Galinsoga_parviflora" title="Galinsoga parviflora">guascas</a></i> (an herb), usually served with sour cream and capers, and accompanied by avocado and rice.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Tamale" title="Tamale">Tamale</a> is a very traditional Bogot&#225; dish. Colombian tamal is a paste made with rice, beef, pork and/or chicken (depending on the region), chickpea, carrot, and spices, wrapped in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Plantain_(cooking)" title="Plantain (cooking)">plantain</a> leaves and steam-cooked.\n</p><p>Figs with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arequipe" title="Arequipe">arequipe</a>, strawberries with cream, <i>postre de natas</i> and <i>cuajada con melao</i> are some of the main desserts offered in the city. <a href="/wiki/Canelazo" title="Canelazo">Canelazo</a> is a hot drink from the Altiplano prepared with <a href="/wiki/Aguapanela" title="Aguapanela">aguapanela</a>, cinnamon and <a href="/wiki/Aguardiente" title="Aguardiente">aguardiente</a>. Another hot beverage is the carajillo, made with coffee (tinto as it is known in Colombia) and aguardiente.\n</p>\n<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ajiaco.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Ajiaco.jpg/240px-Ajiaco.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Ajiaco.jpg/360px-Ajiaco.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Ajiaco.jpg/480px-Ajiaco.jpg 2x" width="160"/></a></div></div>\n<div class="gallerytext">\n<p><a href="/wiki/Ajiaco" title="Ajiaco">Ajiaco</a> is one of the city\'s most representative dishes\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 186px"><div style="width: 186px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 184px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chocolate_Especial.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1288" data-file-width="1975" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Chocolate_Especial.jpg/276px-Chocolate_Especial.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Chocolate_Especial.jpg/414px-Chocolate_Especial.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Chocolate_Especial.jpg/552px-Chocolate_Especial.jpg 2x" width="184"/></a></div></div>\n<div class="gallerytext">\n<p>"Chocolate santafere&#241;o" (Santafe hot chocolate), <a href="/wiki/Almoj%C3%A1bana" title="Almoj&#225;bana">almoj&#225;bana</a>, cheese and <a href="/wiki/Pandebono" title="Pandebono">pandebono</a>\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n</ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Parks_and_recreation">Parks and recreation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Parks and recreation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There are numerous parks in Bogot&#225;, many with facilities for concerts, plays, movies, storytellers and other activities.\n</p>\n<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar_Metropolitan_Park" title="Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var Metropolitan Park">Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var Metropolitan Park</a> is a large park regularly used to stage free concerts (such as the annual <a href="/wiki/Rock_al_Parque" title="Rock al Parque">Rock al Parque</a>, a festival in which popular and/or recently formed international, latinamerican, and Colombian <a href="/wiki/Rock_music" title="Rock music">rock</a> bands play free of charge).</li>\n<li>The public <i>Parque Nacional</i> (National Park) has green spaces, ponds, games for children, foot and bicycle paths, and venues for entertainment such as public screenings of movies and concerts and events organized by the Council of Bogot&#225;</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1_Botanical_Garden" title="Bogot&#225; Botanical Garden">Bogot&#225; Botanical Garden</a> (<i>Jard&#237;n Bot&#225;nico de Bogot&#225;</i>)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/93_Park" title="93 Park">Parque de la 93</a> has day-time leisure activities and nightlife. Several of the top restaurants and bars in the city are in this park, the park is known around the world like the Colombian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pike_Place" title="Pike Place">Pike Place</a> by having the first <a href="/wiki/Starbucks" title="Starbucks">Starbucks</a> in all the country and <a href="/wiki/Carl%27s_Jr." title="Carl\'s Jr.">Carl\'s Jr.</a> as well.</li>\n<li>Mundo Aventura is an <a href="/wiki/Amusement_park" title="Amusement park">amusement park</a>, with an entry charge and charges for the different attractions. It has rides for adults and children, a <a href="/wiki/Petting_zoo" title="Petting zoo">petting zoo</a>, and the "cerdodromo", where pigs race.</li>\n<li>Salitre M&#225;gico is another <a href="/wiki/Amusement_park" title="Amusement park">amusement park</a> with rides and attractions. The park is near the Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var park, where concerts are held throughout the year.</li>\n<li>Parque del Chic&#243; has trees, gardens, artificial creeks and ponds, and a colonial style house converted into a museum; <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Museo_del_Chic%C3%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Museo del Chic&#243; (page does not exist)">Museo del Chic&#243;</a></li>\n<li>To the north of Bogot&#225;, in the municipality of <a href="/wiki/Tocancip%C3%A1" title="Tocancip&#225;">Tocancip&#225;</a>; <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Duque_Park" title="Jaime Duque Park">Jaime Duque Park</a> has rides, a giant map of Colombia, popular exhibits, a zoo, and a big hand holding the world symbolizing God. There is a reproduction of the <a href="/wiki/Taj_Mahal" title="Taj Mahal">Taj Mahal</a> in the park with a collection of reproductions of famous paintings. The park is also used for large concerts, mainly electronic music ones.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Maloka_Museum" title="Maloka Museum">Maloka</a> is an interactive museum of sciences</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1_Savannah_Railway" title="Bogot&#225; Savannah Railway">Tourist train</a> is a sightseeing train, popular with Bogot&#225; residents, which runs to outlying towns <a href="/wiki/Zipaquir%C3%A1" title="Zipaquir&#225;">Zipaquir&#225;</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cajic%C3%A1" title="Cajic&#225;">Cajic&#225;</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nemoc%C3%B3n" title="Nemoc&#243;n">Nemoc&#243;n</a> along the lines of the former <a href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1_Savannah_Railway" title="Bogot&#225; Savannah Railway">Bogot&#225; Savannah Railway</a> on weekends. The route to Zipaquir&#225; (famous for its <a href="/wiki/Salt_Cathedral_of_Zipaquir%C3%A1" title="Salt Cathedral of Zipaquir&#225;">salt cathedral</a>) is 53 kilometres (33 miles) long. Another line goes towards the north for 47&#160;km (29&#160;mi) and ends at <a href="/wiki/Brice%C3%B1o,_Boyac%C3%A1" title="Brice&#241;o, Boyac&#225;">Brice&#241;o</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Usaqu%C3%A9n_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Usaqu&#233;n Park (page does not exist)">Usaqu&#233;n Park</a> is another of the most important parks in the city several of the best restaurants in this city are located there, is recognized to have street performers such as storytellers, magicians, jugglers, etc. and also for being one of the most decorated parks in the city during Christmas time.</li></ul>\n<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lago_del_Parque_Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar.JPG"><img alt="" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="4000" decoding="async" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Lago_del_Parque_Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar.JPG/360px-Lago_del_Parque_Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar.JPG 1.5x, class="gallerytext">\n<p><a href="/wiki/Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar_Park" title="Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var Park">Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var Park</a>\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" park\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px"><div style="width: 162px">\n<div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;"><div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" park\n</p>\n</div>\n</div></li>\n</ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2538" data-file-width="3807" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG/220px-Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG/330px-Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG/440px-Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bogot%C3%A1_Estadio.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Estadio_El_Camp%C3%ADn" title="Estadio El Camp&#237;n">Estadio El Camp&#237;n</a></div></div></div>\n<p>The District Institute for Recreation and Sport promotes recreation, sports and use of the parks in Bogot&#225;.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">Football</a> has been declared a symbol of Bogot&#225;, and is widely played in the city. There are three professional clubs in the city, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Club_Santa_Fe" title="Club Santa Fe">Santa Fe</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Millonarios_F%C3%BAtbol_Club" title="Millonarios F&#250;tbol Club">Millonarios</a>, and <a href="/wiki/La_Equidad" title="La Equidad">La Equidad</a>. The main stadium in the city is The Camp&#237;n Stadium (Estadio Nemesio Camacho El Camp&#237;n) home of the local teams <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Club_Santa_Fe" title="Club Santa Fe">Santa Fe</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Millonarios" title="Millonarios">Millonarios</a>, In 2001 The Camp&#237;n Stadium has been the place for the <a href="/wiki/2001_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2001 Copa Am&#233;rica">2001 Copa Am&#233;rica</a> final between the <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia national football</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico national football</a>, final score 1&#8211;0 in favor of the home team and finally getting their first continental cup. The other soccer venue is the multi-use Techo Metropolitan Stadium which is the home of <a href="/wiki/La_Equidad" title="La Equidad">La Equidad</a>.\n</p><p>Other major sporting venues are the covered Coliseum El Camp&#237;n, the Sim&#243;n Bol&#237;var Aquatic Complex, the Sports Palace, the El Salitre Sports Venue which includes the <a href="/wiki/Luis_Carlos_Gal%C3%A1n_Velodrome" title="Luis Carlos Gal&#225;n Velodrome">Luis Carlos Gal&#225;n Velodrome</a> (which hosted the <a href="/wiki/1995_UCI_Track_Cycling_World_Championships" title="1995 UCI Track Cycling World Championships">1995 UCI Track Cycling World Championships</a>), the El Salitre Diamond Ballpark and the <a href="/wiki/BMX" title="BMX">BMX</a> track "Mario Andr&#233;s Soto".\n</p><p>Bogot&#225; hosted the first Bolivarian Games held in 1938. The city hosted the National Games in 2004, winning the championship. It was a sub-venue Bolivarian Pan American Games. In addition, the city on the route of the Tour of Colombia.\n</p><p>After being a major venue city for the <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2011 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a> that was held in <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>, the Colombian Football Federation announced that Bogot&#225; will be one of the venue cities to host the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Futsal_World_Cup" title="2016 FIFA Futsal World Cup">2016 FIFA Futsal World Cup</a> as well.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports_teams">Sports teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Sports teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table Bogot&#225; (page does not exist)">Bogot&#225; Piratas S.A</a>\n</th>\n<td>Liga DirecTV / Basketball\n</td>\n<td>El Salitre Coliseum\n</td>\n<td>1995\n</td>\n<td>4 (4 <a href="/wiki/Baloncesto_Profesional_Colombiano" title="Baloncesto Profesional Colombiano">copas</a>)\n</td></tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Symbols">Symbols</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Symbols">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The flag originated with the insurgency movement against the colonial authorities which began on 20 July 1810, during which the rebels wore armbands with yellow and red bands, as these colours were those of the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Spain" title="Flag of Spain">Spanish flag</a> used as the flag for the New Kingdom of Granada.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>On 9 October 1952, exactly 142 years after these events, decree 555 of 1952 officially adopted the patriotic armband as the flag of Bogot&#225;.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> The flag of Cundinamarca follows the same pattern, plus a light blue tile which represents the Virgin Mary\'s cape.\n</p><p>The flag itself is a yellow band above a red one. The yellow denotes the gold from the earth, as well as the virtues of justice, clemency, benevolence, the so-called "mundane qualities" (defined as nobility, excellence, richness, generosity, splendour, health, steadfastness, joy and prosperity), long life, eternity, power and constancy. The red denotes the virtue of charity, as well as the qualities of bravery, nobility, values, audacity, victory, honour and furor, Colombians call it the blood of their people.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>The coat of arms of the city was granted by emperor <a href="/wiki/Charles_V,_Holy_Roman_Emperor" title="Charles V, Holy Roman Emperor">Charles V (Charles I of Spain)</a> to the <a href="/wiki/New_Kingdom_of_Granada" title="New Kingdom of Granada">New Kingdom of Granada</a>, by royal decree given in <a href="/wiki/Valladolid" title="Valladolid">Valladolid</a>, Spain on 3 December 1548. It contains a black eagle in the center, which symbolises steadfastness. The eagle is also a symbol of the Habsburgs, which was the ruling family of the Spanish empire at the time. The eagle is crowned with gold and holds a red pomegranate inside a golden background. The border contains olive branches with nine golden pomegranates on a blue background. The two red pomegranates symbolize audacity, and the nine golden ones represent the nine states which constituted the New Kingdom of Granada at the time. In 1932 the coat of arms was officially recognized and adopted as the symbol of Bogot&#225;.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p><p>Bogot&#225;\'s anthem lyrics were written by Pedro Medina Avenda&#241;o; the melody was composed by Roberto Pineda Duque. The song was officially declared the anthem by decree 1000 31 July 1974, by then Mayor of Bogot&#225;, An&#237;bal Fernandez de Soto.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_relations">International relations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: International relations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_twin_towns_and_sister_cities_in_South_America" title="List of twin towns and sister cities in South America">List of twin towns and sister cities in South America</a></div>\n<table class="box-Refimprove_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg"><img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>.
